            |$(0) .
            |          $EXTEND . 
            |. Program Start Address: 000000
            |. Word Count:            016501
            |. In BDI:                000157 (BOOT1)
            |. Bank Starting Address: 000000
            |BSBLK*
            |. 1) SCF (or whatever) does the necessary resets to the hardware components.
            |. 2) SCF sets up B16 and B26 on the boot IP, as well as EX1.
            |. 3) SCF writes ICLP and the Partition Data Bank into main storage
            |.     starting at the specified Initial Load Address.
            |. 4) SCF starts the boot IP.  From the viewpoint of the boot IP, it will
            |.     look like it has received an interrupt.
            |. 5) ICLP loads bootblock from the boot device, and passes control to bootstrap.
            |. 6) Bootstrap loads the OS from the boot device, and passes control to
            |.     Exec initialization.
            |. 7)  Exec initialization initializes the Exec.
            |. 
            |. At a guess, I'd say B2 probably contains ICLP's Level 0 BDT.
=== preceding comment is wrong.
=== I took a look at the code.  It turns out that the contents of B2 are
=== undefined on entry, because the ONVERSION3E folk didn't bother to
=== update the header documentation.  As best I can tell, ICLP is based on
=== B2 for ONVERSION3E machines.  It's not clear why this is the case.
===
=== 0241,,B2:H1 Load path 005=tape, 026=something else
=== 0241,,B2:H2 AND with 0770 != 0430 -> recovery boot, for some reason
=== 0241,,B2:T3 is the UPI for SEND
=== 0243,,B2    is the boot sequence number
===

            |.   least the limits support this address) for hardware read and write.
